# Introduction

Identity and constant function.

  - ``∅ , 1 ∙ "x" ⦂ A  ⊢ ` "x" ⦂ A``
  - ``∅ ⊢ (ƛ "x" ⇒ ` "x") ⦂ [ 1 ∙ A ]⊸ A``
  - ``∅ , 1 ∙ "x" ⦂ A , 0 ∙ "y" ⦂ B ⊢ ` "x" ⦂ A``
  - ``∅ ⊢ (ƛ "x" ⇒ ƛ "y" ⇒ ` "x") ⦂ [ 1 ∙ A ]⊸ [ 0 ∙ B ]⊸ A``

Some numbers.

  - ``∅ , 1 ∙ "z" ⦂ ℕ , 0 ∙ "s" ⦂ [ 1 ∙ ℕ ]⊸ ℕ ⊢ ` "z" ⦂ ℕ``
  - ``∅ , 1 ∙ "z" ⦂ ℕ , 1 ∙ "s" ⦂ [ 1 ∙ ℕ ]⊸ ℕ ⊢ (` "s" · ` "z") ⦂ ℕ``
  - ``∅ , 1 ∙ "z" ⦂ ℕ , ω ∙ "s" ⦂ [ 1 ∙ ℕ ]⊸ ℕ ⊢ (` "s" · (` "s" · ` "z")) ⦂ ℕ``


Words.

    data Mult : Set where
      0# : Mult
      1# : Mult
      ω# : Mult

Words.

    0# + π   =  π
    1# + 1#  =  ω#
    ω# + π   =  ω#

Words.

    0# * π   =  0#
    1# * π   =  π   if  π ≢ 0#
    ω# * π   =  ω#  if  π ≢ 0#

Words.

    0#    1#
      \  /
       ω#

# Contexts

Matrices.

See [this sidenote]({{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative/LinAlg.md%}).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Matrix"></a><a id="2865" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2865" class="Function">Matrix</a> <a id="2872" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2874" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#1726" class="Datatype">Precontext</a> <a id="2885" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2887" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#1726" class="Datatype">Precontext</a> <a id="2898" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2900" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="2904" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2865" class="Function">Matrix</a> <a id="2911" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2911" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="2913" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2913" class="Bound">δ</a> <a id="2915" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2917" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="2919" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2920" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2920" class="Bound">A</a><a id="2921" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2923" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2925" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2911" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="2927" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#1944" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="2929" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2920" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2931" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="2933" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2139" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="2941" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2913" class="Bound">δ</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The identity matrix.

          "x"       "y"       "z"
    "x"  1 ∙ A  ,  0 ∙ B  ,  0 ∙ C
    "y"  0 ∙ A  ,  1 ∙ B  ,  0 ∙ C
    "z"  0 ∙ A  ,  0 ∙ B  ,  1 ∙ C

# Properties of vector operations

Unit scaling does nothing.

  <a id="4032" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4374" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Scaling by a product is the composition of scalings.

Scaling the 0-vector gives the 0-vector.

Scaling by 0 gives the 0-vector.

Adding the 0-vector does nothing.

Vector addition is commutative.

Vector addition is associative.

Scaling by a sum gives the sum of the scalings.

Scaling a sum gives the sum of the scalings.

Adding a row of 0s to the end of the matrix and then multiplying by a vector produces a vector with a 0 at the bottom.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="⊛-zeroʳ"></a><a id="8463" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#8463" class="Function">⊛-zeroʳ</a> <a id="8471" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8473" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="8475" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8476" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#8476" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="8478" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#8478" class="Bound">δ</a><a id="8479" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8481" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8482" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#8482" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="8484" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8486" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2139" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="8494" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#8476" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="8495" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8497" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8498" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#8498" class="Bound">Ξ</a> <a id="8500" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8502" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2865" class="Function">Matrix</a> <a id="8509" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#8476" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="8511" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#8478" class="Bound">δ</a><a id="8512" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8514" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8515" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#8515" class="Bound">B</a><a id="8516" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="8521" class="Comment">---------------------------------------------------</a>
  <a id="8575" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8577" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#8482" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="8579" href="{% endraw %}{{ Linear maps preserve scaling.

id="11212" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2034" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S_</a><a id="11214" class="Symbol">))</a>
  <a id="11219" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4374" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Multiplying by a standard basis vector projects out the corresponding column of the matrix.

  <a id="11993" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4374" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The standard basis vectors put together give the identity matrix.

# Simultaneous Substitution

Extend a matrix as the identity matrix -- add a zero to the end of every row, and add a new row with a 1 and the rest 0s.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="extm"></a><a id="14755" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#14755" class="Function">extm</a> <a id="14760" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14762" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="14764" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14765" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#14765" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="14767" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#14767" class="Bound">δ</a><a id="14768" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="14773" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14775" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2865" class="Function">Matrix</a> <a id="14782" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#14765" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="14784" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#14767" class="Bound">δ</a>
    <a id="14790" class="Comment">--------------------------------</a>
  <a id="14825" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14827" class="Symbol">(∀</a> <a id="14830" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14831" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#14831" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14832" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14834" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14836" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2865" class="Function">Matrix</a> <a id="14843" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14844" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#14765" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="14846" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#1770" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14848" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#14831" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14849" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14851" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14852" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#14767" class="Bound">δ</a> <a id="14854" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#1770" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="14856" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#14831" class="Bound">B</a><a id="14857" class="Symbol">))</a>
